---
title: "SSD科普十六：当 Read Retry 仍然不够时，Soft Read 登场"
date: "2026-06-04 22:37:00"
tags: [SSD, 公众号]
published: true
hideInList: false

<h1 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;" data-pm-slice="0 0 []"><span leaf="">上一篇我们讲了 Read Retry。</span></h1><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">Read Retry 做的事情，本质上是：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">默认 read level 读不出来，那就换一组 read level 再试。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">因为 NAND 里的数据，不是一个干净的 0 或 1，而是一堆 cell 的阈值电压分布。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">SSD 读取数据时，要在两个相邻分布之间放一条判断线。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这条判断线放得合适，读出来的错误 bit 就少。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这条判断线放偏了，原本属于左边状态的 cell，可能被判到右边；原本属于右边状态的 cell，也可能被判到左边。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">所以 Read Retry 的逻辑很直观：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">这条线不行？ 那我换一条线。 还不行？ 那我再换一条线。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">它像是在一片模糊的电压分布里不断调整尺子，试图找到一个更合适的切分位置。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">但这里还有一个更麻烦的问题：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">如果不是判断线放错了，而是两个状态本身已经挤在一起了呢？</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">换句话说，Read Retry 可以解决一部分“线放得不够准”的问题。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">但它不一定能解决“两个分布已经严重重叠”的问题。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">当 Read Retry 仍然不够时，SSD 需要的就不只是“再换一条判断线”。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">它还需要知道：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">这一串读出来的 0 和 1 里面，哪些 bit 最可疑？</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这时候，Soft Read 就该登场了。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem initial;"><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 2rem 0px 0.5rem;padding: 0px;font-family: Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Source Code Pro&quot;, Consolas, Inconsolata, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">一、Read Retry 的极限：换线也救不了所有 bit</span></h2><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">我们可以把两个相邻状态想象成两座山。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">理想情况下，它们中间有一个明显的山谷。</span></p><section style="text-align: center;" nodeleaf=""><img 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">判断线放在山谷中间，左右区分比较清楚。 这个时候，默认 read level 就能比较稳定地把两个状态分开。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">但 NAND 用久之后，情况会变差。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">P/E 次数增加、数据放置时间变长、温度变化、read disturb 累积，都会让这些分布变宽、漂移，甚至互相重叠。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">如果某个 bit 只要 read level 稍微一动，结果就从 1 变成 0，或者从 0 变成 1，说明它就在边界附近。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这个 bit 就值得怀疑。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这就是 Soft Read 要补上的信息。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">它不是重新读出另一份用户数据，而是给原来的 hard data 加上一层判断：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">哪些 bit 比较可靠，哪些 bit 比较可疑。</span></p></blockquote><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium medium;border-style: dashed none none;border-color: rgb(165, 165, 165) currentcolor currentcolor;border-image: initial;height: 1px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 15px;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 2rem 0px 0.5rem;padding: 0px;font-family: Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Source Code Pro&quot;, Consolas, Inconsolata, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, monospace !important;font-weight: 700;color: rgb(248, 95, 72);line-height: 1.35;font-size: 24px;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">三、先看一张 Soft Read 的原理图</span></h2><section style="text-align: center;" nodeleaf=""><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-aistatus="1" data-imgfileid="100000692" data-ratio="1.7777777777777777" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/95znLLjaNf9QMu7X1iaCpbic2OPdEEODJ58Mmicn2sjRibbgSaKlhJCIDKNuhEKbwpShmOKM3qRR9nA0lbyMJsH7fDZibCY15xOtwrqLCYbaEF04/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="720" type="block" src="/post-images/wechat-ssd/ssd-2026-06-04/17844300109630.1257208119390929.jpg"></section><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">如图所示，当相邻状态的阈值电压分布开始重叠时，默认 read level 虽然仍能读出一串 Hard Read 结果，但它并不知道哪些 bit 是“稳的”，哪些 bit 是“擦边猜出来的”。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">Soft Read 的做法，是在默认判断线两侧各再读一次。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">一次用左辅助线。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">一次用右辅助线。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">然后把两次读取结果逐位做&nbsp;</span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;font-weight: bold;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);margin-top: 0px;"><span leaf="">XNOR</span></strong><span leaf="">：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">相同输出 1。 不同输出 0。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这样一来，离边界较远的 bit 会被标记为可靠，而落在重叠区附近的 bit 会被标记为可疑。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">图中间两个 bit，正是因为左右辅助读取结果不同，XNOR 后得到 0，所以它们分别对应“弱 1”和“弱 0”。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 最值得怀疑。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, 要补充的不是“另一个答案”，而是“这个答案的可靠度”。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: 告诉你：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">所以在 状态还没有差到需要动用更复杂的手段。</span></p><h3 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 2rem 0px 0.5rem;padding: 0px;font-family: Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Source Code Pro&quot;, Consolas, Inconsolata, &quot;Ubuntu 不一样。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">普通 Read。 先做 Hard Decode。 成功，就直接返回数据。 失败，再尝试 Read Retry。 仍然困难，再使用 Soft Read。 最后交给 Soft Decode 继续解码。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">所以，Hard Decode 是正常读路径里的主力。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">Soft Decode 更像是错误恢复路径里的重武器。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">平时不用它，是为了速度。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, leaf="">关键时候用它，是为了把数据救回来。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium medium;border-style: dashed none none;border-color: rgb(165, 165, 165) currentcolor currentcolor;border-image: initial;height: 1px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 2rem 0px 0.5rem;padding: 0px;font-family: Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Source Code Pro&quot;, Consolas, Inconsolata, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, monospace initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">九、为什么越到 TLC、QLC，Soft Read 越重要？</span></h2><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">SLC 只有两个状态。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: initial;"><span leaf="">一个状态表示 1，另一个状态表示 0。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: leaf="">两个分布之间距离相对大。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: 个状态。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">QLC 有 16 个状态。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">状态越多，每两个状态之间的间隔就越小。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">可以粗略理解成：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">SLC 是两个山头，中间距离大。 TLC 是八个山头，山头之间更挤。 QLC 是十六个山头，山头之间更挤。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">山头越挤，判断线越难放。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">判断线稍微偏一点，或者分布稍微漂一点，就可能把某些 cell 判错。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这时候，ECC 不仅需要知道：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">这个 bit 是 0 还是 1。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">这个 bit 离边界有多近。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">而 Soft Read 提供的，正是这种“离边界远不远”的信息。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">所以从 SLC 到 MLC、TLC、QLC，NAND 越来越不像一个干净的数字系统。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">它越来越像一个需要统计判断、概率推断和纠错算法一起配合的模拟系统。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这也是为什么现代 SSD 不能只看 NAND。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">更要看 controller、ECC、Read Retry、Vth Tracking、Soft Decode 这些能力。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium medium;border-style: dashed none none;border-color: rgb(165, 165, 165) currentcolor currentcolor;border-image: &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 15px;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, monospace !important;font-weight: 700;color: rgb(248, style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft 和可靠度信息解码。 ECC根据这些信息把数据救回来。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74,
